I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
`createDiffHTML` API fails with "Not a changeset: undefined"
**Description**

I'm encountering a 500 Internal Server Error when calling the `createDiffHTML` API endpoint. Regardless of the startRev and endRev specified, the function fails with the error:

```
[ERROR] API - Error: Not a changeset: undefined
  at PadDiff._createDiffAtext (/run/etherpad-lite/src/node/utils/padDiff.ts:182:15)
  at applyToAText (/run/etherpad-lite/src/static/js/Changeset.ts:1061:9)
  at applyToText (/run/etherpad-lite/src/static/js/Changeset.ts:405:20)
  at async <anonymous> (/run/etherpad-lite/src/node/hooks/express/openapi.ts:679:22)
  at async Object.exports.createDiffHTML (/run/etherpad-lite/src/node/db/API.ts:855:16)
  at async OpenAPIBackend.handleRequest (/run/etherpad-lite/node_modules/.pnpm/openapi-backend@5.11.1/node_modules/openapi-backend/src/7)
  at async PadDiff.getHtml (/run/etherpad-lite/src/node/utils/padDiff.ts:194:19)
  at async handler (/run/etherpad-lite/src/node/hooks/express/openapi.ts:633:20)
  at error (/run/etherpad-lite/src/static/js/Changeset.ts:64:13)
  at process.processTicksAndRejections (node:internal/process/task_queues:95:5)
  at unpack (/run/etherpad-lite/src/static/js/Changeset.ts:363:44)
```

Notably, this even happens if the startRev and endRev are the same. 

This suggests that Etherpad is failing to retrieve or process an expected changeset, even though individual revision changesets are retrievable.

**Steps to Reproduce**

1. Create a new pad.
2. Make a few edits to create multiple revisions.
3. Call the API with:
`GET /api/1.3.0/createDiffHTML?padID=<padID>&startRev=1&endRev=1&apikey=<API_KEY>`
4. The API returns 500 Internal Server Error with `"Not a changeset: undefined"`.
5. Additionally, `createDiffHTML(1,2)` and `createDiffHTML(1,10)` fail, while individual revision changesets (`getRevisionChangeset`) return correctly.

**Expected Behavior**

`createDiffHTML(1,1)` should return valid diff HTML (even if it's an empty or minimal diff).
`createDiffHTML(1,2)` should successfully compute a diff between the first two revisions.

**Actual Behavior**

The API call fails with `"Not a changeset: undefined"`.
Etherpad logs show an error originating from `Changeset.ts`, indicating it is unable to apply or retrieve an expected changeset.

**Server (please complete the following information):**
-  
 - Etherpad version: `2.2.7`
 - API Version: `1.3.0`
 - OS: `Ubuntu 22.04.5 LTS`
 - Node.js version (`node --version`): `v20.18.0`
 - npm version (`npm --version`): `10.8.2`
 - Is the server free of plugins: No. 

**Troubleshooting Done**

✅ Verified individual revision changesets (`getRevisionChangeset`) are retrievable.
✅ Tested smaller revision ranges (`createDiffHTML(1,5)`, `createDiffHTML(1,1)`) — still fails.
✅ Tested on brand new pads — still fails.
✅ Checked the Etherpad GitHub issues (no existing issue found).

**Potential Causes**

- Bug in createDiffHTML Logic?
- Changeset Processing Bug: Etherpad might fail to apply early changesets correctly.
- Revision 0 Issue: The initial changeset might not be properly interpreted when computing diffs.


</pr_description>

    17	class PadDiff {
    18	  private readonly _pad: PadType;
    19	    private readonly _fromRev: string;
    20	    private readonly _toRev: string;

    23	    private self: PadDiff | undefined
    24	  constructor(pad: PadType, fromRev:string, toRev:string) {
    25	    // check parameters
    26	    if (!pad || !pad.id || !pad.atext || !pad.pool) {
    27	      throw new Error('Invalid pad');
    28	    }
    29	
    30	    const range = pad.getValidRevisionRange(fromRev, toRev);
    31	    if (!range) throw new Error(`Invalid revision range. startRev: ${fromRev} endRev: ${toRev}`);
    32	
    33	    this._pad = pad;
    34	    this._fromRev = range.startRev;
    35	    this._toRev = range.endRev;
    36	    this._html = null;
    37	    this._authors = [];
    38	  }
    39	  _isClearAuthorship(changeset: any){
    40	    // unpack
    41	    const unpacked = unpack(changeset);
    42	
    43	    // check if there is nothing in the charBank
    44	    if (unpacked.charBank !== '') {
    45	      return false;
    46	    }
    47	
    48	    // check if oldLength == newLength
    49	    if (unpacked.oldLen !== unpacked.newLen) {
    50	      return false;
    51	    }
    52	
    53	    const [clearOperator, anotherOp] = deserializeOps(unpacked.ops);
    54	
    55	    // check if there is only one operator
    56	    if (anotherOp != null) return false;
    57	
    58	    // check if this operator doesn't change text
    59	    if (clearOperator.opcode !== '=') {
    60	      return false;
    61	    }
    62	
    63	    // check that this operator applys to the complete text
    64	    // if the text ends with a new line, its exactly one character less, else it has the same length
    65	    if (clearOperator.chars !== unpacked.oldLen - 1 && clearOperator.chars !== unpacked.oldLen) {
    66	      return false;
    67	    }
    68	
    69	    const [appliedAttribute, anotherAttribute] =
    70	        attributes.attribsFromString(clearOperator.attribs, this._pad.pool);
    71	
    72	    // Check that the operation has exactly one attribute.
    73	    if (appliedAttribute == null || anotherAttribute != null) return false;
    74	
    75	    // check if the applied attribute is an anonymous author attribute
    76	    if (appliedAttribute[0] !== 'author' || appliedAttribute[1] !== '') {
    77	      return false;
    78	    }
    79	
    80	    return true;
    81	  }
    82	  async _createClearAuthorship(rev: any){
    83	    const atext = await this._pad.getInternalRevisionAText(rev);
    84	
    85	    // build clearAuthorship changeset
    86	    const builder = new Builder(atext.text.length);
    87	    builder.keepText(atext.text, [['author', '']], this._pad.pool);
    88	    const changeset = builder.toString();
    89	
    90	    return changeset;
    91	  }
    92	
    93	  async _createClearStartAtext(rev: any){
    94	    // get the atext of this revision
    95	    const atext = await this._pad.getInternalRevisionAText(rev);
    96	
    97	    // create the clearAuthorship changeset
    98	    const changeset = await this._createClearAuthorship(rev);
    99	
   100	    // apply the clearAuthorship changeset
   101	    const newAText = applyToAText(changeset, atext, this._pad.pool);
   102	
   103	    return newAText;
   104	  }
   105	  async _getChangesetsInBulk(startRev: any, count: any) {
   106	    // find out which revisions we need
   107	    const revisions = [];
   108	    for (let i = startRev; i < (startRev + count) && i <= this._pad.head; i++) {
   109	      revisions.push(i);
   110	    }
   111	
   112	    // get all needed revisions (in parallel)
   113	    const changesets:any[] = [];
   114	    const authors: any[] = [];
   115	    await Promise.all(revisions.map((rev) => this._pad.getRevision(rev).then((revision) => {
   116	      const arrayNum = rev - startRev;
   117	      changesets[arrayNum] = revision.changeset;
   118	      authors[arrayNum] = revision.meta.author;
   119	    })));
   120	
   121	    return {changesets, authors};
   122	  }
   123	  _addAuthors(authors: PadAuthor[]){
   124	      this.self = this;
   125	
   126	    // add to array if not in the array
   127	    authors.forEach((author) => {
   128	      if (this.self!._authors.indexOf(author) === -1) {
   129	        this.self!._authors.push(author);
   130	      }
   131	    });
   132	  }
   133	  async _createDiffAtext(){
   134	    const bulkSize = 100;
   135	
   136	    // get the cleaned startAText
   137	    let atext = await this._createClearStartAtext(this._fromRev);
   138	
   139	    let superChangeset = null;
   140	
   141	    for (let rev = this._fromRev + 1; rev <= this._toRev; rev += bulkSize) {
   142	      // get the bulk
   143	      const {changesets, authors} = await this._getChangesetsInBulk(rev, bulkSize);
   144	
   145	      const addedAuthors = [];
   146	
   147	      // run through all changesets
   148	      for (let i = 0; i < changesets.length && (rev + i) <= this._toRev; ++i) {
   149	        let changeset = changesets[i];
   150	
   151	        // skip clearAuthorship Changesets
   152	        if (this._isClearAuthorship(changeset)) {
   153	          continue;
   154	        }
   155	
   156	        changeset = this._extendChangesetWithAuthor(changeset, authors[i], this._pad.pool);
   157	
   158	        // add this author to the authorarray
   159	        addedAuthors.push(authors[i]);
   160	
   161	        // compose it with the superChangset
   162	        if (superChangeset == null) {
   163	          superChangeset = changeset;
   164	        } else {
   165	          superChangeset = compose(superChangeset, changeset, this._pad.pool);
   166	        }
   167	      }
   168	
   169	      // add the authors to the PadDiff authorArray
   170	      this._addAuthors(addedAuthors);
   171	    }
   172	
   173	    // if there are only clearAuthorship changesets, we don't get a superChangeset,
   174	    // so we can skip this step
   175	    if (superChangeset) {
   176	      const deletionChangeset = this._createDeletionChangeset(superChangeset, atext, this._pad.pool);
   177	
   178	      // apply the superChangeset, which includes all addings
   179	      atext = applyToAText(superChangeset, atext, this._pad.pool);
   180	
   181	      // apply the deletionChangeset, which adds a deletions
   182	      atext = applyToAText(deletionChangeset, atext, this._pad.pool);
   183	    }
   184	
   185	    return atext;
   186	  }
   187	  async getHtml(){
   188	    // cache the html
   189	    if (this._html != null) {
   190	      return this._html;
   191	    }
   192	
   193	    // get the diff atext
   194	    const atext = await this._createDiffAtext();
   195	
   196	    // get the authorColor table
   197	    const authorColors = await this._pad.getAllAuthorColors();
   198	
   199	    // convert the atext to html
   200	    this._html = await exportHtml.getHTMLFromAtext(this._pad, atext, authorColors);
   201	
   202	    return this._html;
   203	  }
   204	
   205	  async getAuthors() {
   206	    // check if html was already produced, if not produce it, this generates
   207	    // the author array at the same time
   208	    if (this._html == null) {
   209	      await this.getHtml();
   210	    }
   211	
   212	    return this.self!._authors;
   213	  }
   214	
   215	  _extendChangesetWithAuthor(changeset: any, author: any, apool: any){
   216	    // unpack
   217	    const unpacked = unpack(changeset);
   218	
   219	    const assem = new OpAssembler();
   220	
   221	    // create deleted attribs
   222	    const authorAttrib = apool.putAttrib(['author', author || '']);
   223	    const deletedAttrib = apool.putAttrib(['removed', true]);
   224	    const attribs = `*${numToString(authorAttrib)}*${numToString(deletedAttrib)}`;
   225	
   226	    for (const operator of deserializeOps(unpacked.ops)) {
   227	      if (operator.opcode === '-') {
   228	        // this is a delete operator, extend it with the author
   229	        operator.attribs = attribs;
   230	      } else if (operator.opcode === '=' && operator.attribs) {
   231	        // this is operator changes only attributes, let's mark which author did that
   232	        operator.attribs += `*${numToString(authorAttrib)}`;
   233	      }
   234	
   235	      // append the new operator to our assembler
   236	      assem.append(operator);
   237	    }
   238	
   239	    // return the modified changeset
   240	    return pack(unpacked.oldLen, unpacked.newLen, assem.toString(), unpacked.charBank);
   241	  }
   242	  _createDeletionChangeset(cs: any, startAText: any, apool: any){
   243	    const lines = splitTextLines(startAText.text);
   244	    const alines = splitAttributionLines(startAText.attribs, startAText.text);
   245	
   246	    // lines and alines are what the exports is meant to apply to.
   247	    // They may be arrays or objects with .get(i) and .length methods.
   248	    // They include final newlines on lines.
   249	
   250	    const linesGet = (idx: number) => {
   251	      // @ts-ignore
   252	      if (lines.get) {
   253	        // @ts-ignore
   254	        return lines.get(idx);
   255	      } else {
   256	        // @ts-ignore
   257	        return lines[idx];
   258	      }
   259	    };

   309	          if (curLineOpsNext!.done) {
   310	            curLineNextOp = new Op();
   311	          } else {
   312	            curLineNextOp = curLineOpsNext!.value;
   313	            curLineOpsNext = curLineOps!.next();
   314	          }
   315	        }
   316	
   317	        const charsToUse = Math.min(numChars, curLineNextOp.chars);
   318	
   319	        func(charsToUse, curLineNextOp.attribs,
   320	            charsToUse === curLineNextOp.chars && curLineNextOp.lines > 0);
   321	        numChars -= charsToUse;
   322	        curLineNextOp.chars -= charsToUse;
   323	        curChar += charsToUse;
   324	      }
   325	
   326	      if (!curLineNextOp.chars && curLineOpsNext!.done) {
   327	        curLine++;
   328	        curChar = 0;
   329	      }
   330	    };
   331	
   332	    const skip = (N:number, L:number) => {
   333	      if (L) {
   334	        curLine += L;
   335	        curChar = 0;
   336	      } else if (curLineOps && curLineOpsLine === curLine) {
   337	        consumeAttribRuns(N, () => {});
   338	      } else {
   339	        curChar += N;
   340	      }
   341	    };
   342	
   343	    const nextText = (numChars: number) => {
   344	      let len = 0;
   345	      const assem = new StringAssembler();
   346	      const firstString = linesGet(curLine).substring(curChar);
   347	      len += firstString.length;
   348	      assem.append(firstString);
   349	
   350	      let lineNum = curLine + 1;
   351	
   352	      while (len < numChars) {
   353	        const nextString = linesGet(lineNum);
   354	        len += nextString.length;
   355	        assem.append(nextString);
   356	        lineNum++;
   357	      }
   358	
   359	      return assem.toString().substring(0, numChars);
   360	    };
   361	
   362	    const cachedStrFunc = (func:Function) => {
   363	      const cache:MapArrayType<any> = {};
   364	
   365	      return (s:string) => {
   366	        if (!cache[s]) {
   367	          cache[s] = func(s);
   368	        }
   369	        return cache[s];
   370	      };
   371	    };
   372	
   373	    for (const csOp of deserializeOps(unpacked.ops)) {
   374	      if (csOp.opcode === '=') {
   375	        const textBank = nextText(csOp.chars);
   376	
   377	        // decide if this equal operator is an attribution change or not.
   378	        // We can see this by checkinf if attribs is set.
   379	        // If the text this operator applies to is only a star,
   380	        // than this is a false positive and should be ignored
   381	        if (csOp.attribs && textBank !== '*') {
   382	          const attribs = AttributeMap.fromString(csOp.attribs, apool);
   383	          const undoBackToAttribs = cachedStrFunc((oldAttribsStr: string) => {
   384	            const oldAttribs = AttributeMap.fromString(oldAttribsStr, apool);
   385	            const backAttribs = new AttributeMap(apool)
   386	                .set('author', '')
   387	                .set('removed', 'true');
   388	            for (const [key, value] of attribs) {
   389	              const oldValue = oldAttribs.get(key);
   390	              if (oldValue !== value) backAttribs.set(key, oldValue);
   391	            }
   392	            // TODO: backAttribs does not restore removed attributes (it is missing attributes that
   393	            // are in oldAttribs but not in attribs). I don't know if that is intentional.
   394	            return backAttribs.toString();
   395	          });
   396	
   397	          let textLeftToProcess = textBank;
   398	
   399	          while (textLeftToProcess.length > 0) {
   400	            // process till the next line break or process only one line break
   401	            let lengthToProcess = textLeftToProcess.indexOf('\n');
   402	            let lineBreak = false;
   403	            switch (lengthToProcess) {
   404	              case -1:
   405	                lengthToProcess = textLeftToProcess.length;
   406	                break;
   407	              case 0:
   408	                lineBreak = true;
   409	                lengthToProcess = 1;
   410	                break;
   411	            }
   412	
   413	            // get the text we want to procceed in this step
   414	            const processText = textLeftToProcess.substr(0, lengthToProcess);
   415	
   416	            textLeftToProcess = textLeftToProcess.substr(lengthToProcess);
   417	
   418	            if (lineBreak) {
   419	              builder.keep(1, 1); // just skip linebreaks, don't do a insert + keep for a linebreak
   420	
   421	              // consume the attributes of this linebreak
   422	              consumeAttribRuns(1, () => {});
   423	            } else {
   424	              // add the old text via an insert, but add a deletion attribute +
   425	              // the author attribute of the author who deleted it
   426	              let textBankIndex = 0;
   427	              consumeAttribRuns(lengthToProcess, (len: number, attribs:string, endsLine: string) => {
   428	                // get the old attributes back
   429	                const oldAttribs = undoBackToAttribs(attribs);
   430	
   431	                builder.insert(processText.substr(textBankIndex, len), oldAttribs);
   432	                textBankIndex += len;
   433	              });
   434	
   435	              builder.keep(lengthToProcess, 0);
   436	            }
   437	          }
   438	        } else {
   439	          skip(csOp.chars, csOp.lines);
   440	          builder.keep(csOp.chars, csOp.lines);
   441	        }
   442	      } else if (csOp.opcode === '+') {
   443	        builder.keep(csOp.chars, csOp.lines);
   444	      } else if (csOp.opcode === '-') {
   445	        const textBank = nextText(csOp.chars);
   446	        let textBankIndex = 0;
   447	
   448	        consumeAttribRuns(csOp.chars, (len: number, attribs: string[], endsLine: string) => {
   449	          builder.insert(textBank.substr(textBankIndex, len), attribs + csOp.attribs);
   450	          textBankIndex += len;
   451	        });
   452	      }
   453	    }
   454	
   455	    return checkRep(builder.toString());
   456	  }
   457	
   458	}
   459	
   460	
   461	// this method is 80% like Changeset.inverse. I just changed so instead of reverting,
   462	// it adds deletions and attribute changes to the atext.
   463	// @ts-ignore
   464	PadDiff.prototype._createDeletionChangeset = function (cs, startAText, apool) {
   465	
   466	};
   467	
   468	// export the constructor
   469	module.exports = PadDiff;
   470

    97	  async appendRevision(aChangeset:string, authorId = '') {
    98	    const newAText = applyToAText(aChangeset, this.atext, this.pool);
    99	    if (newAText.text === this.atext.text && newAText.attribs === this.atext.attribs &&
   100	        this.head !== -1) {
   101	      return this.head;
   102	    }
   103	    copyAText(newAText, this.atext);
   104	
   105	    const newRev = ++this.head;
   106	
   107	    // ex. getNumForAuthor
   108	    if (authorId !== '') this.pool.putAttrib(['author', authorId]);
   109	
   110	    const hook = this.head === 0 ? 'padCreate' : 'padUpdate';
   111	    await Promise.all([
   112	      // @ts-ignore
   113	      this.db.set(`pad:${this.id}:revs:${newRev}`, {
   114	        changeset: aChangeset,
   115	        meta: {
   116	          author: authorId,
   117	          timestamp: Date.now(),
   118	          ...newRev === this.getKeyRevisionNumber(newRev) ? {
   119	            pool: this.pool,
   120	            atext: this.atext,
   121	          } : {},
   122	        },
   123	      }),
   124	      this.saveToDatabase(),
   125	      authorId && authorManager.addPad(authorId, this.id),
   126	      hooks.aCallAll(hook, {
   127	        pad: this,
   128	        authorId,
   129	        get author() {
   130	          pad_utils.warnDeprecated(`${hook} hook author context is deprecated; use authorId instead`);
   131	          return this.authorId;
   132	        },
   133	        set author(authorId) {
   134	          pad_utils.warnDeprecated(`${hook} hook author context is deprecated; use authorId instead`);
   135	          this.authorId = authorId;
   136	        },
   137	        ...this.head === 0 ? {} : {
   138	          revs: newRev,
   139	          changeset: aChangeset,
   140	        },
   141	      }),
   142	    ]);
   143	    return newRev;
   144	  }
   145	
   146	  toJSON() {
   147	    const o:Pad = {...this, pool: this.pool.toJsonable()};
   148	    // @ts-ignore
   149	    delete o.db;
   150	    // @ts-ignore
   151	    delete o.id;
   152	    return o;
   153	  }
   154	
   155	  // save all attributes to the database
   156	  async saveToDatabase() {
   157	    // @ts-ignore
   158	    await this.db.set(`pad:${this.id}`, this);
   159	  }
   160	
   161	  // get time of last edit (changeset application)
   162	  async getLastEdit() {
   163	    const revNum = this.getHeadRevisionNumber();
   164	    // @ts-ignore
   165	    return await this.db.getSub(`pad:${this.id}:revs:${revNum}`, ['meta', 'timestamp']);
   166	  }
   167	
   168	  async getRevisionChangeset(revNum: number) {
   169	    // @ts-ignore
   170	    return await this.db.getSub(`pad:${this.id}:revs:${revNum}`, ['changeset']);
   171	  }
   172	
   173	  async getRevisionAuthor(revNum: number) {
   174	    // @ts-ignore
   175	    return await this.db.getSub(`pad:${this.id}:revs:${revNum}`, ['meta', 'author']);
   176	  }
   177	
   178	  async getRevisionDate(revNum: number) {
   179	    // @ts-ignore
   180	    return await this.db.getSub(`pad:${this.id}:revs:${revNum}`, ['meta', 'timestamp']);
   181	  }
   182	
   183	  /**
   184	   * @param {number} revNum - Must be a key revision number (see `getKeyRevisionNumber`).
   185	   * @returns The attribute text stored at `revNum`.
   186	   */
   187	  async _getKeyRevisionAText(revNum: number) {
   188	    // @ts-ignore
   189	    return await this.db.getSub(`pad:${this.id}:revs:${revNum}`, ['meta', 'atext']);
   190	  }
   191	
   192	  /**
   193	   * Returns all authors that worked on this pad
   194	   * @return {[String]} The id of authors who contributed to this pad
   195	   */
   196	  getAllAuthors() {
   197	    const authorIds = [];
   198	
   199	    for (const key in this.pool.numToAttrib) {
   200	      if (this.pool.numToAttrib[key][0] === 'author' && this.pool.numToAttrib[key][1] !== '') {
   201	        authorIds.push(this.pool.numToAttrib[key][1]);
   202	      }
   203	    }
   204	
   205	    return authorIds;
   206	  }
   207	
   208	  async getInternalRevisionAText(targetRev: number) {
   209	    const keyRev = this.getKeyRevisionNumber(targetRev);
   210	    const headRev = this.getHeadRevisionNumber();
   211	    if (targetRev > headRev) targetRev = headRev;
   212	    const [keyAText, changesets] = await Promise.all([
   213	      this._getKeyRevisionAText(keyRev),
   214	      Promise.all(
   215	          Stream.range(keyRev + 1, targetRev + 1).map(this.getRevisionChangeset.bind(this))),
   216	    ]);
   217	    const apool = this.apool();
   218	    let atext = keyAText;
   219	    for (const cs of changesets) atext = applyToAText(cs, atext, apool);
   220	    return atext;
   221	  }
   222	
   223	  async getRevision(revNum: number) {
   224	    return await this.db.get(`pad:${this.id}:revs:${revNum}`);
   225	  }
   226	
   227	  async getAllAuthorColors() {
   228	    const authorIds = this.getAllAuthors();
   229	    const returnTable:MapArrayType<string> = {};
   230	    const colorPalette = authorManager.getColorPalette();
   231	
   232	    await Promise.all(
   233	        authorIds.map((authorId) => authorManager.getAuthorColorId(authorId).then((colorId:string) => {
   234	          // colorId might be a hex color or an number out of the palette
   235	          returnTable[authorId] = colorPalette[colorId] || colorId;
   236	        })));
   237	
   238	    return returnTable;
   239	  }
   240	
   241	  getValidRevisionRange(startRev: any, endRev:any) {
   242	    startRev = parseInt(startRev, 10);
   243	    const head = this.getHeadRevisionNumber();
   244	    endRev = endRev ? parseInt(endRev, 10) : head;
   245	
   246	    if (isNaN(startRev) || startRev < 0 || startRev > head) {
   247	      startRev = null;
   248	    }
   249	
   250	    if (isNaN(endRev) || endRev < startRev) {
   251	      endRev = null;
   252	    } else if (endRev > head) {
   253	      endRev = head;
   254	    }
   255	
   256	    if (startRev != null && endRev != null) {
   257	      return {startRev, endRev};
   258	    }
   259	    return null;
   260	  }
   261	
   262	  getKeyRevisionNumber(revNum: number) {
   263	    return Math.floor(revNum / 100) * 100;
   264	  }
   265	
   266	  /**
   267	   * @returns {string} The pad's text.
   268	   */
   269	  text(): string {
   270	    return this.atext.text;
   271	  }
   272	
   273	  /**
   274	   * Splices text into the pad. If the result of the splice does not end with a newline, one will be
   275	   * automatically appended.
   276	   *
   277	   * @param {number} start - Location in pad text to start removing and inserting characters. Must
   278	   *     be a non-negative integer less than or equal to `this.text().length`.
   279	   * @param {number} ndel - Number of characters to remove starting at `start`. Must be a
   280	   *     non-negative integer less than or equal to `this.text().length - start`.
   281	   * @param {string} ins - New text to insert at `start` (after the `ndel` characters are deleted).
   282	   * @param {string} [authorId] - Author ID of the user making the change (if applicable).
   283	   */
   284	  async spliceText(start:number, ndel:number, ins: string, authorId: string = '') {
   285	    if (start < 0) throw new RangeError(`start index must be non-negative (is ${start})`);
   286	    if (ndel < 0) throw new RangeError(`characters to delete must be non-negative (is ${ndel})`);
   287	    const orig = this.text();
   288	    assert(orig.endsWith('\n'));
   289	    if (start + ndel > orig.length) throw new RangeError('start/delete past the end of the text');
   290	    ins = exports.cleanText(ins);

    22	import {MapArrayType} from "../types/MapType";
    23	import {PadType} from "../types/PadType";
    24	
    25	const CustomError = require('../utils/customError');
    26	const Pad = require('../db/Pad');
    27	const db = require('./DB');
    28	import settings from '../utils/Settings';
    29	
    30	/**
    31	 * A cache of all loaded Pads.
    32	 *
    33	 * Provides "get" and "set" functions,
    34	 * which should be used instead of indexing with brackets. These prepend a
    35	 * colon to the key, to avoid conflicting with built-in Object methods or with
    36	 * these functions themselves.
    37	 *
    38	 * If this is needed in other places, it would be wise to make this a prototype
    39	 * that's defined somewhere more sensible.
    40	 */
    41	const globalPads:MapArrayType<any> = {
    42	  get(name: string)
    43	  {
    44	    return this[`:${name}`];
    45	    },
    46	  set(name: string, value: any)
    47	  {
    48	    this[`:${name}`] = value;
    49	  },
    50	  remove(name: string) {
    51	    delete this[`:${name}`];
    52	  },
    53	};
    54	
    55	/**
    56	 * A cache of the list of all pads.
    57	 *
    58	 * Updated without db access as new pads are created/old ones removed.
    59	 */
    60	const padList = new class {
    61	  private _cachedList: string[] | null;
    62	    private _list: Set<string>;
    63	    private _loaded: Promise<void> | null;
    64	  constructor() {
    65	    this._cachedList = null;
    66	    this._list = new Set();
    67	    this._loaded = null;
    68	  }
    69	
    70	  /**
    71	   * Returns all pads in alphabetical order as array.
    72	   * @returns {Promise<string[]>} A promise that resolves to an array of pad IDs.
    73	   */
    74	  async getPads() {
    75	    if (!this._loaded) {
    76	      this._loaded = (async () => {
    77	        const dbData = await db.findKeys('pad:*', '*:*:*');
    78	        if (dbData == null) return;
    79	        for (const val of dbData) this.addPad(val.replace(/^pad:/, ''));
    80	      })();
    81	    }
    82	    await this._loaded;
    83	    if (!this._cachedList) this._cachedList = [...this._list].sort();
    84	    return this._cachedList;
    85	  }
    86	
    87	  addPad(name: string) {
    88	    if (this._list.has(name)) return;
    89	    this._list.add(name);
    90	    this._cachedList = null;
    91	  }
    92	
    93	  removePad(name: string) {
    94	    if (!this._list.has(name)) return;
    95	    this._list.delete(name);
    96	    this._cachedList = null;
    97	  }
    98	}();
    99	
   100	// initialises the all-knowing data structure
   101	
   102	/**
   103	 * Returns a Pad Object with the callback
   104	 * @param id A String with the id of the pad
   105	 * @param {string} [text] - Optional initial pad text if creating a new pad.
   106	 * @param {string} [authorId] - Optional author ID of the user that initiated the pad creation (if
   107	 *     applicable).
   108	 */
   109	exports.getPad = async (id: string, text?: string|null, authorId:string|null = ''):Promise<PadType> => {
   110	  // check if this is a valid padId
   111	  if (!exports.isValidPadId(id)) {
   112	    throw new CustomError(`${id} is not a valid padId`, 'apierror');
   113	  }
   114	
   115	  // check if this is a valid text
   116	  if (text != null) {
   117	    // check if text is a string
   118	    if (typeof text !== 'string') {
   119	      throw new CustomError('text is not a string', 'apierror');
   120	    }
   121	
   122	    // check if text is less than 100k chars
   123	    if (text.length > 100000) {
   124	      throw new CustomError('text must be less than 100k chars', 'apierror');
   125	    }
   126	  }
   127	
   128	  let pad = globalPads.get(id);
   129	
   130	  // return pad if it's already loaded
   131	  if (pad != null) {
   132	    return pad;
   133	  }
   134	
   135	  // try to load pad
   136	  pad = new Pad.Pad(id);
   137	
   138	  // initialize the pad
   139	  await pad.init(text, authorId);
   140	  globalPads.set(id, pad);
   141	  padList.addPad(id);
   142	
   143	  return pad;
   144	};
   145	
   146	exports.listAllPads = async () => {
   147	  const padIDs = await padList.getPads();
   148	
   149	  return {padIDs};
   150	};
   151	
   152	
   153	
   154	
   155	// checks if a pad exists
   156	exports.doesPadExist = async (padId: string) => {
   157	  const value = await db.get(`pad:${padId}`);
   158	
   159	  return (value != null && value.atext);
   160	};
   161	
   162	// alias for backwards compatibility
   163	exports.doesPadExists = exports.doesPadExist;
   164	
   165	/**
   166	 * An array of padId transformations. These represent changes in pad name policy over
   167	 * time, and allow us to "play back" these changes so legacy padIds can be found.
   168	 */
   169	const padIdTransforms = [
   170	  [/\s+/g, '_'],
   171	  [/:+/g, '_'],
   172	];
   173	
   174	// returns a sanitized padId, respecting legacy pad id formats
   175	exports.sanitizePadId = async (padId: string) => {
   176	  for (let i = 0, n = padIdTransforms.length; i < n; ++i) {
   177	    const exists = await exports.doesPadExist(padId);
   178	
   179	    if (exists) {
   180	      return padId;
   181	    }
   182	
   183	    const [from, to] = padIdTransforms[i];
   184	
   185	    // @ts-ignore
   186	    padId = padId.replace(from, to);
   187	  }
   188	
   189	  if (settings.lowerCasePadIds) padId = padId.toLowerCase();
   190	
   191	  // we're out of possible transformations, so just return it
   192	  return padId;
   193	};
   194	
   195	exports.isValidPadId = (padId: string) => /^(g.[a-zA-Z0-9]{16}\$)?[^$]{1,50}$/.test(padId);
   196	
   197	/**
   198	 * Removes the pad from database and unloads it.
   199	 */
   200	exports.removePad = async (padId: string) => {
   201	  const p = db.remove(`pad:${padId}`);
   202	  exports.unloadPad(padId);
   203	  padList.removePad(padId);
   204	  await p;
   205	};
   206	
   207	// removes a pad from the cache
   208	exports.unloadPad = (padId: string) => {
   209	  globalPads.remove(padId);
   210	};

   291	    const willEndWithNewline =
   292	        start + ndel < orig.length || // Keeping last char (which is guaranteed to be a newline).
   293	        ins.endsWith('\n') ||
   294	        (!ins && start > 0 && orig[start - 1] === '\n');

   302	   * Replaces the pad's text with new text.
   303	   *
   304	   * @param {string} newText - The pad's new text. If this string does not end with a newline, one
   305	   *     will be automatically appended.

   309	  async setText(newText: string, authorId = '') {
   310	    await this.spliceText(0, this.text().length, newText, authorId);

   313	  /**

   320	  async appendText(newText:string, authorId = '') {

   324	  /**
   325	   * Adds a chat message to the pad, including saving it to the database.
   326	   *
   327	   * @param {(ChatMessage|string)} msgOrText - Either a chat message object (recommended) or a
   328	   *     string containing the raw text of the user's chat message (deprecated).
   329	   * @param {?string} [authorId] - The user's author ID. Deprecated; use `msgOrText.authorId`
   330	   *     instead.
   331	   * @param {?number} [time] - Message timestamp (milliseconds since epoch). Deprecated; use
   332	   *     `msgOrText.time` instead.
   333	   */
   334	  async appendChatMessage(msgOrText: string| ChatMessage, authorId = null, time = null) {
   335	    const msg =
   336	          msgOrText instanceof ChatMessage ? msgOrText : new ChatMessage(msgOrText, authorId, time);
   337	    this.chatHead++;
   338	    await Promise.all([
   339	      // Don't save the display name in the database because the user can change it at any time. The
   340	      // `displayName` property will be populated with the current value when the message is read
   341	      // from the database.
   342	      this.db.set(`pad:${this.id}:chat:${this.chatHead}`, {...msg, displayName: undefined}),
   343	      this.saveToDatabase(),
   344	    ]);
   345	  }
   346	
   347	  /**
   348	   * @param {number} entryNum - ID of the desired chat message.
   349	   * @returns {?ChatMessage}
   350	   */
   351	  async getChatMessage(entryNum: number) {
   352	    const entry = await this.db.get(`pad:${this.id}:chat:${entryNum}`);
   353	    if (entry == null) return null;
   354	    const message = ChatMessage.fromObject(entry);
   355	    message.displayName = await authorManager.getAuthorName(message.authorId);
   356	    return message;
   357	  }
   358	
   359	  /**
   360	   * @param {number} start - ID of the first desired chat message.
   361	   * @param {number} end - ID of the last desired chat message.
   362	   * @returns {ChatMessage[]} Any existing messages with IDs between `start` (inclusive) and `end`
   363	   *     (inclusive), in order. Note: `start` and `end` form a closed interval, not a half-open
   364	   *     interval as is typical in code.
   365	   */
   366	  async getChatMessages(start: string, end: number) {
   367	    const entries =
   368	        await Promise.all(Stream.range(start, end + 1).map(this.getChatMessage.bind(this)));
   369	
   370	    // sort out broken chat entries
   371	    // it looks like in happened in the past that the chat head was
   372	    // incremented, but the chat message wasn't added
   373	    return entries.filter((entry) => {
   374	      const pass = (entry != null);
   375	      if (!pass) {
   376	        console.warn(`WARNING: Found broken chat entry in pad ${this.id}`);
   377	      }
   378	      return pass;
   379	    });
   380	  }
   381	
   382	  async init(text:string, authorId = '') {
   383	    // try to load the pad
   384	    const value = await this.db.get(`pad:${this.id}`);
   385	
   386	    // if this pad exists, load it
   387	    if (value != null) {
   388	      Object.assign(this, value);
   389	      if ('pool' in value) this.pool = new AttributePool().fromJsonable(value.pool);
   390	    } else {
   391	      if (text == null) {
   392	        const context = {pad: this, authorId, type: 'text', content: settings.defaultPadText};
   393	        await hooks.aCallAll('padDefaultContent', context);
   394	        if (context.type !== 'text') throw new Error(`unsupported content type: ${context.type}`);
   395	        text = exports.cleanText(context.content);
   396	      }
   397	      const firstChangeset = makeSplice('\n', 0, 0, text);
   398	      await this.appendRevision(firstChangeset, authorId);
   399	    }
   400	    await hooks.aCallAll('padLoad', {pad: this});
   401	  }

    41	export const generateJWTToken =  () => {
    42	  const jwt = new SignJWT({
    43	    sub: 'admin',
    44	    jti: '123',
    45	    exp: Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000) + 60 * 60,
    46	    aud: 'account',
    47	    iss: 'http://localhost:9001',
    48	    admin: true
    49	  })
    50	  jwt.setProtectedHeader({alg: 'RS256'})
    51	  return jwt.sign(privateKeyExported!)
    52	}

   100	  });

   106	/**
   107	 * Waits for the next named socket.io event. Rejects if there is an error event while waiting
   108	 * (unless waiting for that error event).
   109	 *
   110	 * @param {io.Socket} socket - The socket.io Socket object to listen on.
   111	 * @param {string} event - The socket.io Socket event to listen for.
   112	 * @returns The argument(s) passed to the event handler.
   113	 */
   114	export const waitForSocketEvent = async (socket: any, event:string) => {
   115	  const errorEvents = [
   116	    'error',
   117	    'connect_error',
   118	    'connect_timeout',
   119	    'reconnect_error',
   120	    'reconnect_failed',
   121	  ];
   122	  const handlers = new Map();
   123	  let cancelTimeout;
   124	  try {
   125	    const timeoutP = new Promise<void>((resolve, reject) => {
   126	      const timeout = setTimeout(() => {
   127	        reject(new Error(`timed out waiting for ${event} event`));
   128	        cancelTimeout = () => {};
   129	      }, 1000);
   130	      cancelTimeout = () => {
   131	        clearTimeout(timeout);
   132	        resolve();
   133	        cancelTimeout = () => {};
   134	      };
   135	    });
   136	    const errorEventP = Promise.race(errorEvents.map((event) => new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
   137	      handlers.set(event, (errorString:string) => {
   138	        logger.debug(`socket.io ${event} event: ${errorString}`);
   139	        reject(new Error(errorString));
   140	      });
   141	    })));
   142	    const eventP = new Promise<string|string[]>((resolve) => {
   143	      // This will overwrite one of the above handlers if the user is waiting for an error event.
   144	      handlers.set(event, (...args:string[]) => {
   145	        logger.debug(`socket.io ${event} event`);
   146	        if (args.length > 1) return resolve(args);
   147	        resolve(args[0]);
   148	      });
   149	    });
   150	    for (const [event, handler] of handlers) socket.on(event, handler);
   151	    // timeoutP and errorEventP are guaranteed to never resolve here (they can only reject), so the
   152	    // Promise returned by Promise.race() is guaranteed to resolve to the eventP value (if
   153	    // the event arrives).
   154	    return await Promise.race([timeoutP, errorEventP, eventP]);
   155	  } finally {
   156	    cancelTimeout!();
   157	    for (const [event, handler] of handlers) socket.off(event, handler);
   158	  }
   159	};
   160	
   161	/**
   162	 * Establishes a new socket.io connection.
   163	 *
   164	 * @param {object} [res] - Optional HTTP response object. The cookies from this response's
   165	 *     `set-cookie` header(s) are passed to the server when opening the socket.io connection. If
   166	 *     nullish, no cookies are passed to the server.
   167	 * @returns {io.Socket} A socket.io client Socket object.
   168	 */
   169	export const connect = async (res:any = null) => {
   170	  // Convert the `set-cookie` header(s) into a `cookie` header.
   171	  const resCookies = (res == null) ? {} : setCookieParser.parse(res, {map: true});
   172	  const reqCookieHdr = Object.entries(resCookies).map(
   173	      // @ts-ignore
   174	      ([name, cookie]) => `${name}=${encodeURIComponent(cookie.value)}`).join('; ');
   175	
   176	  logger.debug('socket.io connecting...');
   177	  let padId = null;
   178	  if (res) {
   179	    padId = res.req.path.split('/p/')[1];
   180	  }

    99	const removeSignalListener = (signal: NodeJS.Signals, listener: any) => {
   100	  logger.debug(`Removing ${signal} listener because it might interfere with shutdown tasks. ` +
   101	               `Function code:\n${listener.toString()}\n` +
   102	               `Current stack:\n${new Error()!.stack!.split('\n').slice(1).join('\n')}`);
   103	  process.off(signal, listener);

   107	let startDoneGate: Gate<unknown>
   108	exports.start = async () => {
   109	  switch (state) {
   110	    case State.INITIAL:
   111	      break;
   112	    case State.STARTING:
   113	      await startDoneGate;
   114	      // Retry. Don't fall through because it might have transitioned to STATE_TRANSITION_FAILED.
   115	      return await exports.start();
   116	    case State.RUNNING:
   117	      return express.server;
   118	    case State.STOPPING:
   119	    case State.STOPPED:
   120	    case State.EXITING:
   121	    case State.WAITING_FOR_EXIT:
   122	    case State.STATE_TRANSITION_FAILED:
   123	      throw new Error('restart not supported');
   124	    default:
   125	      throw new Error(`unknown State: ${state.toString()}`);
   126	  }
   127	  logger.info('Starting Etherpad...');
   128	  startDoneGate = new Gate();
   129	  state = State.STARTING;
   130	  try {
   131	    // Check if the Etherpad version is up to date
   132	    check();
   133	
   134	    // @ts-ignore
   135	    stats.gauge('memoryUsage', () => process.memoryUsage().rss);

   167	
   168	  // say goodbye if this is an unknown function

   178	    if (fields.apikey !== apikey!.trim()) {

require('tsx/cjs');

(async () => {
  const settings = require('./src/node/utils/Settings').default;
  settings.dbType = 'dirty';
  settings.dbSettings = {filename: ':memory:'};
  settings.ip = 'localhost';
  settings.port = 0;

  const db = require('./src/node/db/DB');
  const padManager = require('./src/node/db/PadManager');
  const API = require('./src/node/db/API');
  const hooks = require('./src/static/js/pluginfw/hooks');

  await db.init();
  await hooks.aCallAll('loadSettings', {settings});

  const padId = `diff-repro-${Date.now()}`;
  const pad = await padManager.getPad(padId, 'hello');
  await pad.appendText(' world', 'a.author1');
  await pad.appendText('!', 'a.author2');

  console.log('head', pad.getHeadRevisionNumber());
  console.log('rev1 changeset', await pad.getRevisionChangeset(1));

  for (const [startRev, endRev] of [[1, 1], [1, 2]]) {
    try {
      const result = await API.createDiffHTML(padId, startRev, endRev);
      console.log(`createDiffHTML(${startRev},${endRev}) ok`, {
        htmlLength: result.html.length,
        authors: result.authors,
      });
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(`createDiffHTML(${startRev},${endRev}) failed:`, err && (err.stack || err.message || err));
      process.exitCode = 1;
    }
  }

  await db.shutdown();
})();
EOF

    23	  constructor(pad: PadType, fromRev:string, toRev:string) {
    24	    // check parameters
    25	    if (!pad || !pad.id || !pad.atext || !pad.pool) {
    26	      throw new Error('Invalid pad');
    27	    }
    28	
    29	    const range = pad.getValidRevisionRange(fromRev, toRev);
    30	    if (!range) throw new Error(`Invalid revision range. startRev: ${fromRev} endRev: ${toRev}`);
    31	
    32	    this._pad = pad;
    33	    this._fromRev = range.startRev;
    34	    this._toRev = range.endRev;
    35	    this._html = null;
    36	    this._authors = [];
    37	  }
    38	  _isClearAuthorship(changeset: any){
    39	    // unpack
    40	    const unpacked = unpack(changeset);
    41	
    42	    // check if there is nothing in the charBank
    43	    if (unpacked.charBank !== '') {
    44	      return false;
    45	    }
    46	
    47	    // check if oldLength == newLength
    48	    if (unpacked.oldLen !== unpacked.newLen) {
    49	      return false;
    50	    }
    51	
    52	    const [clearOperator, anotherOp] = deserializeOps(unpacked.ops);
    53	
    54	    // check if there is only one operator
    55	    if (anotherOp != null) return false;
    56	
    57	    // check if this operator doesn't change text
    58	    if (clearOperator.opcode !== '=') {
    59	      return false;
    60	    }
    61	
    62	    // check that this operator applys to the complete text
    63	    // if the text ends with a new line, its exactly one character less, else it has the same length
    64	    if (clearOperator.chars !== unpacked.oldLen - 1 && clearOperator.chars !== unpacked.oldLen) {
    65	      return false;
    66	    }
    67	
    68	    const [appliedAttribute, anotherAttribute] =
    69	        attributes.attribsFromString(clearOperator.attribs, this._pad.pool);
    70	
    71	    // Check that the operation has exactly one attribute.
    72	    if (appliedAttribute == null || anotherAttribute != null) return false;
    73	
    74	    // check if the applied attribute is an anonymous author attribute
    75	    if (appliedAttribute[0] !== 'author' || appliedAttribute[1] !== '') {
    76	      return false;
    77	    }
    78	
    79	    return true;
    80	  }
    81	  async _createClearAuthorship(rev: any){
    82	    const atext = await this._pad.getInternalRevisionAText(rev);
    83	
    84	    // build clearAuthorship changeset
    85	    const builder = new Builder(atext.text.length);
    86	    builder.keepText(atext.text, [['author', '']], this._pad.pool);
    87	    const changeset = builder.toString();
    88	
    89	    return changeset;
    90	  }
    91	
    92	  async _createClearStartAtext(rev: any){
    93	    // get the atext of this revision
    94	    const atext = await this._pad.getInternalRevisionAText(rev);
    95	
    96	    // create the clearAuthorship changeset
    97	    const changeset = await this._createClearAuthorship(rev);
    98	
    99	    // apply the clearAuthorship changeset
   100	    const newAText = applyToAText(changeset, atext, this._pad.pool);
   101	
   102	    return newAText;
   103	  }
   104	  async _getChangesetsInBulk(startRev: any, count: any) {
   105	    // find out which revisions we need
   106	    const revisions = [];
   107	    for (let i = startRev; i < (startRev + count) && i <= this._pad.head; i++) {
   108	      revisions.push(i);
   109	    }
   110	
   111	    // get all needed revisions (in parallel)
   112	    const changesets:any[] = [];
   113	    const authors: any[] = [];
   114	    await Promise.all(revisions.map((rev) => this._pad.getRevision(rev).then((revision) => {
   115	      const arrayNum = rev - startRev;
   116	      changesets[arrayNum] = revision.changeset;
   117	      authors[arrayNum] = revision.meta.author;
   118	    })));
   119	
   120	    return {changesets, authors};
   121	  }
   122	  _addAuthors(authors: PadAuthor[]){
   123	    // add to array if not in the array
   124	    authors.forEach((author) => {
   125	      if (this._authors.indexOf(author) === -1) {
   126	        this._authors.push(author);
   127	      }
   128	    });
   129	  }
   130	  async _createDiffAtext(){
   131	    const bulkSize = 100;
   132	
   133	    // get the cleaned startAText
   134	    let atext = await this._createClearStartAtext(this._fromRev);
   135	
   136	    let superChangeset = null;
   137	
   138	    for (let rev = this._fromRev + 1; rev <= this._toRev; rev += bulkSize) {
   139	      // get the bulk
   140	      const {changesets, authors} = await this._getChangesetsInBulk(rev, bulkSize);
   141	
   142	      const addedAuthors = [];
   143	
   144	      // run through all changesets
   145	      for (let i = 0; i < changesets.length && (rev + i) <= this._toRev; ++i) {
   146	        let changeset = changesets[i];

   148	        // skip clearAuthorship Changesets
   149	        if (this._isClearAuthorship(changeset)) {
   150	          continue;
   151	        }
   152	
   153	        changeset = this._extendChangesetWithAuthor(changeset, authors[i], this._pad.pool);
   154	
   155	        // add this author to the authorarray

   157	
   158	        // compose it with the superChangset
   159	        if (superChangeset == null) {
   160	          superChangeset = changeset;
   161	        } else {
   162	          superChangeset = compose(superChangeset, changeset, this._pad.pool);
   163	        }
   164	      }
   165	
   166	      // add the authors to the PadDiff authorArray
   167	      this._addAuthors(addedAuthors);
   168	    }
   169	
   170	    // if there are only clearAuthorship changesets, we don't get a superChangeset,
   171	    // so we can skip this step
   172	    if (superChangeset) {
   173	      const deletionChangeset = this._createDeletionChangeset(superChangeset, atext, this._pad.pool);
   174	
   175	      // apply the superChangeset, which includes all addings
   176	      atext = applyToAText(superChangeset, atext, this._pad.pool);
   177	
   178	      // apply the deletionChangeset, which adds a deletions
   179	      atext = applyToAText(deletionChangeset, atext, this._pad.pool);
   180	    }
   181	
   182	    return atext;
   183	  }
   184	  async getHtml(){
   185	    // cache the html
   186	    if (this._html != null) {
   187	      return this._html;
   188	    }
   189

   192	
   193	    // get the authorColor table
   194	    const authorColors = await this._pad.getAllAuthorColors();
   195	
   196	    // convert the atext to html
   197	    this._html = await exportHtml.getHTMLFromAtext(this._pad, atext, authorColors);
   198	
   199	    return this._html;
   200	  }

   207	    }

   209	    return this._authors;

+    hooks.aCallAll
+      basic behavior
+        ✔ calls all asynchronously, returns values in order
+        ✔ passes hook name
+        ✔ undefined context -> {}
+        ✔ null context -> {}
+        ✔ context unmodified
+      aCallAll callback
+        ✔ exception in callback rejects
+        ✔ propagates error on exception
+        ✔ propagages null error on success
+        ✔ propagages results on success
+        ✔ returns callback return value
+      result processing
+        ✔ no registered hooks (undefined) -> []
+        ✔ no registered hooks (empty list) -> []
+        ✔ flattens one level
+        ✔ filters out undefined
+        ✔ preserves null
+        ✔ all undefined -> []
+    hooks.callAllSerial
+      basic behavior
+        ✔ calls all asynchronously, serially, in order
+        ✔ passes hook name
+        ✔ undefined context -> {}
+        ✔ null context -> {}
+        ✔ context unmodified
+      result processing
+        ✔ no registered hooks (undefined) -> []
+        ✔ no registered hooks (empty list) -> []
+        ✔ flattens one level
+        ✔ filters out undefined
+        ✔ preserves null
+        ✔ all undefined -> []
+    hooks.aCallFirst
+      ✔ no registered hooks (undefined) -> []
+      ✔ no registered hooks (empty list) -> []
+      ✔ passes hook name => {}
+      ✔ undefined context => {}
+      ✔ null context => {}
+      ✔ context unmodified
